id="cm-content" class="cm-content"><div class="cm-container"><div class="cm-row"><div id="cm-primary" class="cm-primary"><div class="cm-posts" class="clearfix"><article sdfdfds id="post-29218" class="post-29218 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-japanese-vocabulary category-top-view"><div class="cm-post-content"><div class="cm-entry-header-meta"><div class="cm-post-categories"><a href="https://learnjapanesedaily.com/japanese-vocabulary" rel="category tag">Japanese vocabulary</a><a href="https://learnjapanesedaily.com/top-view" style="background:#ffffff" rel="category tag">top view</a></div></div><div class="cm-entry-summary"><div class="code-block code-block-5" style="margin: 8px 0; clear: both;"> </div><h1 style="text-align: center;">1000 most common japanese words list<img decoding="async" class="aligncenter wp-image-2398 " src="https://learnjapanesedaily.com/wp-content/uploads/tu-vung-tieng-nhat.jpg" alt width="263" height="158" /></h1><p style="text-align: justify;">1000 most common japanese words list. Each language has about 3000 core words that are used in 70% of daily conversation. In this post, Learn Japanese daily would like to provide you 1000 most common japanese words. The list is divided in to each 10, so that you can learn it everyday with 10 word, and each page have 60 words for you to learn everyweek.</p><div id="toc_container" class="toc_light_blue no_bullets"><p class="toc_title">Contents</p><ul class="toc_list"><li><a href="#1000_most_common_japanese_words_8211_week_2"><span class="toc_number toc_depth_1">1</span> 1000 most common japanese words &#8211; week 2</a><ul><li><ul><li><a href="#Day_7"><span class="toc_number toc_depth_3">1.0.1</span> Day 7</a></li><li><a href="#Day_8"><span class="toc_number toc_depth_3">1.0.2</span> Day 8</a></li><li><a href="#Day_9"><span class="toc_number toc_depth_3">1.0.3</span> Day 9</a></li><li><a href="#Day_10"><span class="toc_number toc_depth_3">1.0.4</span> Day 10</a></li><li><a href="#Day_11"><span class="toc_number toc_depth_3">1.0.5</span> Day 11</a></li><li><a href="#Day_12"><span class="toc_number toc_depth_3">1.0.6</span> Day 12</a></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></div><h2><span id="1000_most_common_japanese_words_8211_week_2">1000 most common japanese words &#8211; week 2</span></h2><h4><span id="Day_7">Day 7</span></h4><p>61. 住む (sumu) : live, reside</p><p>62. 働く (hataraku) : work</p><p>63. 難しい (muzukashii) : difficult</p><p>64. 先生 (sensei) : teacher</p><p>65. 立つ (tatsu) : stand, rise</p><p>66. 呼ぶ (yobu) : call, name</p><p>67. 大学 (daigaku) : university, college</p><p>68. 安い (yasui) : cheap, inexpensive</p><p>69. もっと (motto) : more</p><p>70. 帰る (kaeru) : go back home</p><h4><span id="Day_8">Day 8</span></h4><p>71. 分かる (wakaru) : understand</p><p>72. 広い (hiroi) : wide, big</p><p>73. 数 (suu) : number</p><p>74. 近い (chikai) : near, close</p><p>75. そこ (soko) : there</p><p>76. 走る (hashiru) : run</p><p>77. 入れる (ireru) : put in</p><p>78. 教える (oshieru) : teach, tell</p><div class="code-block code-block-1" style="margin: 8px 0; clear: both;"> <ins class="adsbygoogle" style="display:block" data-ad-client="ca-pub-4869892931320660" data-ad-slot="4800397836" data-ad-format="auto" data-full-width-responsive="true"></ins> <script type="0abc9438cfded5c6b9e8a642-text/javascript">(adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});</script></div><p>79. 歩く (aruku) : walk, go on foot</p><p>80. 会う (au) : meet</p><h4><span id="Day_9">Day 9</span></h4><p>81. 書く (kaku) : write</p><p>82. 頭 (atama) : head</p><p>83. 売る (uru) : sell</p><p>84. 大好き (daisuki) : like (something) a lot</p><p>85. 体 (karada) : body, physique</p><p>86. 直ぐ (sugu) : at once, soon</p><p>87. 飛ぶ (tobu) : fly</p><p>88. とても (totemo) : very (colloquial)</p><p>89. 誰 (dare) : who</p><p>90. 好き (suki) : favorite, liked</p><h4><span id="Day_10">Day 10</span></h4><p>91. 読む (yomu) : read</p><p>92. 次 (tsugi) : next</p><p>93. あなた (anata) : you</p><p>94. 飲む (nomu) : drink</p><p>95. 古い (furui) : old</p><p>96. 質問 (shitsumon) : question</p><p>97. 今日 (kyou) : today (colloquial)</p><p>98. 友達 (tomodachi) : friend, companion (colloquial)</p><p>99. 早い (hayai) : early</p><p>100. どれ (dore) : what, which</p><h4><span id="Day_11">Day 11</span></h4><p>101. 美しい (utsukushii) : beautiful</p><p>102. いつも (itsumo) : always (colloquial)</p><p>103. 足 (ashi) : leg, foot</p><p>104. 起こす (okosu) : wake (someone) up</p><p>105. 見せる (miseru) : show</p><p>106. 娘 (musume) : daughter, girl</p><p>107. 楽しむ (tanoshimu) : enjoy</p><p>108. 色 (iro) : color</p><p>109. みんな (minna) : everybody (colloquial)</p><p>110. 取る (toru) : take, get</p><h4><span id="Day_12">Day 12</span></h4><p>111. 勉強 (benkyou) : study</p><p>112. できる (dekiru) : can do, be good at</p><p>113. 短い (mijikai) : short, brief</p><p>114. 落ちる (ochiru) : fall, come down</p><p>115. 息子 (musuko) : son</p><p>116. 白い (shiroi) : white, blank</p><p>117. 飛行機 (hikouki) : airplane</p><p>118. 病気 (byouki) : illness</p><p>119. 冬 (fuyu) : winter</p><p>120. 年 (toshi) : year, age</p><p style="text-align: right;"><em>&#8211;&gt; see more at next page</em></p> <ins
